These are formatted for forum use. [img=https://dl.dropboxusercontent.com/s/k4uc8x303juelvt/linked%20files.png'] can be posted at the top of the list. Roms used to make the set can be labeled using [img=https://dl.dropboxusercontent.com/s/fyxuz94r550kvvo/main.png] Standard placement is between the [b] and the filename. Entries that have more than one rom linked may be numbered for clarity. You may look up existing forum posts for reference. 


The older emulator sometimes calculated patched roms differently than the file. This seems to have changed with the new ralibretro. This was rarely an issue an may no longer apply with the current tools.
